<!-- ====================== SCRIPT CORREGIDO ====================== -->
<script type='module'>
//<![CDATA[
  import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/12.11.0/firebase-app.js";
  import { getFirestore, collection, addDoc, serverTimestamp, query, where, getDocs } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/12.11.0/firebase-firestore.js";
  import { getAuth, signInWithEmailAndPassword, onAuthStateChanged } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/12.11.0/firebase-auth.js";

  const firebaseConfig = {
    apiKey: "AIzaSyDA6mRLGymepNx3EXoCOH7CUiBXd6syGeg",
    authDomain: "sign-in-method-b7675.firebaseapp.com",
    projectId: "sign-in-method-b7675",
    storageBucket: "sign-in-method-b7675.firebasestorage.app",
    messagingSenderId: "713340652755",
    appId: "1:713340652755:web:57fc07b795dc503391d826",
    measurementId: "G-E7C8KNRSSZ"
  };

  const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
  const db = getFirestore(app);
  const auth = getAuth(app);

  let currentUser = null;
  let isFavorited = false;

  // ==================== LOCALSTORAGE ====================
  function saveCredentials(email, password) {
    localStorage.setItem("email", email);
    localStorage.setItem("password", password);
  }
  function clearCredentials() {
    localStorage.removeItem("email");
    localStorage.removeItem("password");
  }

  // ==================== AUTO-LOGIN ====================
  async function tryAutoLogin() {
    const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    let email = params.get("email");
    let password = params.get("pass");
    if (!email || !password) {
      email = localStorage.getItem("email");
      password = localStorage.getItem("password");
    }
    if (!email || !password) return false;

    try {
      await signInWithEmailAndPassword(auth, email, password);
      saveCredentials(email, password);
      const cleanUrl = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname + window.location.hash;
      window.history.replaceState({}, document.title, cleanUrl);
      return true;
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("Autologin falló:", e);
      clearCredentials();
      return false;
    }
  }

  // ==================== TOAST (actualizado con clase .show) ====================
  function showToast(message) {
    const toast = document.createElement("div");
    toast.className = "fav-toast";
    toast.textContent = message;
    document.body.appendChild(toast);

    requestAnimationFrame(() => toast.classList.add("show"));

    setTimeout(() => {
      toast.classList.remove("show");
      setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 300);
    }, 2800);
  }

  // ==================== VERIFICAR FAVORITO ====================
  async function checkIfFavorited(user) {
    if (!user) return false;
    const currentUrl = window.location.href;
    const q = query(
      collection(db, `users/${user.uid}/favorites`),
      where("url", "==", currentUrl)
    );
    const snapshot = await getDocs(q);
    return !snapshot.empty;
  }

  // ==================== ESTADO DEL BOTÓN ====================
  function updateButtonState() {
    const btn = document.getElementById("floating-fav-btn");
    if (!btn) return;
    if (isFavorited) {
      btn.classList.add("favorited");
      btn.title = "Ya está en tus favoritos";
    } else {
      btn.classList.remove("favorited");
      btn.title = "Guardar en favoritos";
    }
  }

  // ==================== EXTRAER DATOS (sin cambios) ====================
  function getCurrentContentData() {
    const typeDiv = document.querySelector('div[data-post-type]');
    let type = typeDiv ? typeDiv.getAttribute('data-post-type') : 'unknown';
    let title = document.title;
    let poster = "";
    const synopsisEl = document.getElementById('tmdb-synopsis');
    const synopsis = synopsisEl ? synopsisEl.textContent.trim() : '';
    const url = window.location.href;

    if (type === 'episode') {
      const headerTitle = document.querySelector('.post-header__title');
      const serieName = headerTitle ? headerTitle.textContent.trim() : '';
      const seasonEl = document.querySelector('.post-header__meta .ssn');
      const episodeEl = document.querySelector('.post-header__meta .num');
      const season = seasonEl ? seasonEl.textContent.trim() : '';
      const episodeNum = episodeEl ? episodeEl.textContent.trim() : '';
      if (serieName) title = `${serieName} - ${season} ${episodeNum}`;

      const episodeDiv = document.querySelector('div[data-backdrop]');
      if (episodeDiv) {
        poster = episodeDiv.getAttribute('data-backdrop') || episodeDiv.getAttribute('data-player-backdrop') || "";
      }
      if (!poster) {
        const hiddenImg = document.querySelector('div[data-post-type="episode"] img');
        if (hiddenImg) poster = hiddenImg.src;
      }

      return {
        title, poster, url, year: "—", synopsis, rating: "", duration: "", type: "episode",
        season: episodeDiv ? episodeDiv.getAttribute('data-season-number') : '',
        episode: episodeDiv ? episodeDiv.getAttribute('data-episode-count') : '',
        serieName: serieName,
        serieUrl: episodeDiv ? episodeDiv.getAttribute('data-serie-url') : '',
        savedAt: serverTimestamp()
      };
    }

    const titleLi = document.querySelector('ul.post-details li[data]');
    if (titleLi) title = titleLi.getAttribute('data') || title;
    const hiddenImg = document.querySelector('div[data-post-type] img');
    if (hiddenImg) poster = hiddenImg.src;
    const ul = document.querySelector('ul.post-details');
    if (!poster && ul) poster = ul.getAttribute('data-backdrop') || ul.getAttribute('data-player-backdrop') || "";

    let year = "Desconocido";
    const yearLi = document.querySelector('ul.post-details li[data-year]');
    if (yearLi) year = yearLi.getAttribute('data-year');
    let rating = ul ? ul.getAttribute('data-imdb') || "" : "";
    let duration = "";
    const durationLi = document.querySelector('ul.post-details li[data-duration]');
    if (durationLi) duration = durationLi.getAttribute('data-duration');

    return { title, poster, url, year, synopsis, rating, duration, type, savedAt: serverTimestamp() };
  }

  // ==================== GUARDAR FAVORITO ====================
  async function saveToFavorites() {
    let user = auth.currentUser || currentUser;
    if (!user) {
      const loginUrl = "https://lzrdrz10.github.io/log/";
      const returnTo = encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);
      window.location.href = `${loginUrl}?returnTo=${returnTo}`;
      return;
    }
    if (isFavorited) {
      showToast("✅ Ya está en tus favoritos");
      return;
    }

    const data = getCurrentContentData();
    try {
      await addDoc(collection(db, `users/${user.uid}/favorites`), data);
      isFavorited = true;
      updateButtonState();
      showToast(`✅ ${data.title} guardado en favoritos!`);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
      showToast("❌ Error al guardar en Firebase");
    }
  }

  // ==================== INICIO (CORREGIDO) ====================
  window.addEventListener("load", async () => {
    await tryAutoLogin();

    // ←←← ESTO ES LO QUE ARREGLA EL ERROR ←←←
    onAuthStateChanged(auth, async (user) => {
      currentUser = user;
      if (user) {
        isFavorited = await checkIfFavorited(user);
      } else {
        isFavorited = false;
      }
      updateButtonState();
    });

    const btn = document.getElementById("floating-fav-btn");
    if (btn) btn.addEventListener("click", saveToFavorites);
  });
//]]>
</script>

          <b:include data='{ icon: &quot;search&quot; }' name='i:meteor'/>

  <script>
document.addEventListener(&quot;DOMContentLoaded&quot;, function () {
    const searchInput = document.querySelector(&quot;.search__field input&quot;);
    const searchWrapper = document.querySelector(&quot;.search__wrapper&quot;);
    const searchResults = document.createElement(&quot;div&quot;);
    searchResults.className = &quot;live-results&quot;;
    searchWrapper.appendChild(searchResults);

    let searchTimeout;

    searchInput.addEventListener(&quot;input&quot;, function () {
        clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
        const query = searchInput.value.trim().toLowerCase();
        
        if (!query) {
            searchResults.innerHTML = &quot;&quot;;
            searchResults.classList.remove(&quot;is-show&quot;);
            return;
        }

        searchTimeout = setTimeout(async () =&gt; {
            searchResults.innerHTML = &quot;&lt;span class=&#39;search-spinner&#39;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&quot;;
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/feeds/posts/summary?alt=json&amp;q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&amp;max-results=5`);
                const data = await response.json();
                const entries = data.feed.entry || [];
                
                searchResults.innerHTML = entries.length ? entries.map(entry =&gt; {
                    const title = entry.title.$t;
                    const link = entry.link.find(l =&gt; l.rel === &quot;alternate&quot;).href;
                    const thumbnail = entry.media$thumbnail?.url || &quot;https://i.imgur.com/kQxzAj0.jpeg&quot;;
                    return `&lt;a class=&#39;result-item&#39; href=&#39;${link}&#39;&gt;
                       <!-- &lt;img class=&#39;result-thumbnail&#39; src=&#39;${thumbnail}&#39; alt=&#39;thumbnail&#39;&gt; -->
                        &lt;span class=&#39;result-title&#39;&gt;彡 ${title}&lt;/span&gt;
                    &lt;/a&gt;`;
                }).join(&quot;&quot;) : &quot;&lt;div class=&#39;no-results&#39;&gt;No se encontraron resultados.&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;
                
                searchResults.classList.add(&quot;is-show&quot;);
            } catch (error) {
                searchResults.innerHTML = &quot;&lt;div class=&#39;error-message&#39;&gt;Error al buscar. Intenta nuevamente.&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;
            }
        }, 300);
    });

    document.addEventListener(&quot;click&quot;, function (event) {
        if (!searchWrapper.contains(event.target)) {
            searchResults.classList.remove(&quot;is-show&quot;);
        }
    });
});

</script>

<style>
.snow-container {
  position: fixed;
  top: 0;
  left: 0;
  width: 100%;
  height: 100%;
  pointer-events: none;
  z-index: 9999;
  overflow: hidden;

/* Copo */
.snowflake {
  position: absolute;
  top: -20px;
  opacity: 0;
  will-change: transform, opacity;
  animation: fall linear forwards;
}

/* Animación completa */
@keyframes fall {
  0% {
    transform: translateY(0) translateX(0) rotate(0deg);
    opacity: 0;
  }
  10% {
    opacity: 1;
  }
  80% {
    opacity: 1;
  }
  100% {
    transform: translateY(110vh) translateX(var(--drift)) rotate(360deg);
    opacity: 0;
  }
}
</style>


<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {

  const container = document.querySelector('.snow-container');
  if (!container) return;

  const maxFlakes = 40; // 🔥 máximo en pantalla (fluido)
  let currentFlakes = 0;

  function createSnowflake() {

    if (currentFlakes >= maxFlakes) return;

    const snowflake = document.createElement('img');
    snowflake.src = 'https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhrCP7D7FkgUvs_D0BJTtUmYZ_DZ4Z_Qb2pf_DoEJOz8zKurx2sOXw2WrAeGubbOtKajvJTPOdZ_y4rjTbJokjWJBcaVgpsHPEzkrhJi4_CzbjyMbZV8YO8flX8-hvhmgNuTlKGdb_yR3o02vtuxfMuKhrNObvGUYRpr1TnFh3MHX2istPVt4yzwrqNjmIS/s1600/PLAYA-BALON.png';

    snowflake.classList.add('snowflake');

    // Posición horizontal aleatoria
    snowflake.style.left = Math.random() * 100 + 'vw';

    // Tamaño
    snowflake.style.width = (Math.random() * 15 + 10) + 'px';

    // Duración (velocidad)
    const duration = Math.random() * 5 + 6;
    snowflake.style.animationDuration = duration + 's';

    // Movimiento lateral
    const drift = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 100;
    snowflake.style.setProperty('--drift', drift + 'px');

    container.appendChild(snowflake);
    currentFlakes++;

    // 🔥 eliminar cuando termina
    setTimeout(() => {
      snowflake.remove();
      currentFlakes--;
    }, duration * 1000);
  }

  // 🔄 Generación continua (natural)
  setInterval(() => {
    createSnowflake();
  }, 400); // frecuencia (puedes bajar a 300 si quieres más nieve)

});
</script>]]></b:widget-setting>

<script>
// 🔹 Activar link actual
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const currentUrl = window.location.href.replace(/\/$/, '');
    const menuLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.menu-link');

    menuLinks.forEach(link => {
        if (!link.hasAttribute('href')) return;

        let linkUrl = link.getAttribute('href').replace(/\/$/, '');

        if (linkUrl === 'https://www.lzplayhd.xyz') {
            if (currentUrl === linkUrl) {
                link.classList.add('active');
            }
        } else {
            if (currentUrl === linkUrl || currentUrl.includes(linkUrl)) {
                link.classList.add('active');
            }
        }
    });
});


// 🔥 Ocultar / mostrar con scroll
let lastScrollTop = 0;
const bottomBar = document.querySelector('.bottom-bar');

window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
    let currentScroll = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;

    if (currentScroll > lastScrollTop && currentScroll > 50) {
        bottomBar.style.transform = "translateY(120%)";
        bottomBar.style.opacity = "0";
    } else {
        bottomBar.style.transform = "translateY(0)";
        bottomBar.style.opacity = "1";
    }

    lastScrollTop = currentScroll <= 0 ? 0 : currentScroll;
});
</script>]]></b:widget-setting>

  const duration = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement)
                    .getPropertyValue("--preloader-time")
                    .trim();

  // Convierte el valor de CSS (ej: "4s") a milisegundos
  const ms = parseFloat(duration) * (duration.includes("ms") ? 1 : 1000);

  setTimeout(() => {
    preloader.classList.add("hide");
  }, ms);

   <script>
document.addEventListener(&quot;DOMContentLoaded&quot;, function () {
    // Configuraciones ajustables
    const config = {
        speed: 8, // Velocidad de caída (segundos, mayor = más lento)
        quantity: 50, // Cantidad de copos visibles en simultáneo
        sizeRange: [15, 35], // Rango de tamaño en píxeles [min, max]
        types: [&#39;balanceo&#39;], // Tipos de caída disponibles: &#39;balanceo&#39;
    };

    const snowContainer = document.getElementById(&quot;snow-container&quot;);

    // Función para ajustar la altura del contenedor al tamaño de la ventana
    function adjustSnowContainerHeight() {
        const windowHeight = window.innerHeight; // Alto de la ventana visible
        snowContainer.style.height = `${windowHeight * 2}px`; // Doble la altura de la ventana
    }

    // Llamada inicial para ajustar la altura
    adjustSnowContainerHeight();

    // Asegurarse de que la altura se ajuste también cuando el usuario haga scroll o redimensione la ventana
    window.addEventListener(&quot;resize&quot;, adjustSnowContainerHeight);

    // Crear un copo de nieve con configuración específica
    function createSnowflake() {
        const snowflake = document.createElement(&quot;div&quot;);
        snowflake.classList.add(&quot;snowflake&quot;);
        snowflake.style.left = Math.random() * 100 + &quot;%&quot;;
        snowflake.style.animationDuration = config.speed + Math.random() * 2 + &quot;s&quot;; // Duración con variación
        snowflake.style.width = snowflake.style.height = Math.random() * 
            (config.sizeRange[1] - config.sizeRange[0]) + config.sizeRange[0] + &quot;px&quot;;

        // Determinar tipo de caída
        if (config.types.includes(&#39;balanceo&#39;)) {
            snowflake.style.animationName = &quot;fall&quot;;
        }

        snowContainer.appendChild(snowflake);

        // Eliminar el copo una vez termine su animación
        snowflake.addEventListener(&quot;animationend&quot;, () =&gt; {
            snowflake.remove();
        });
    }

    // Generar copos a intervalos controlados
    setInterval(() =&gt; {
        const currentSnowflakes = document.querySelectorAll(&quot;.snowflake&quot;).length;
        if (currentSnowflakes &lt; config.quantity) {
            createSnowflake();
        }
    }, 200); // Intervalo de creación
});

    </script>
<script>
    document.addEventListener(&quot;DOMContentLoaded&quot;, function () {
        const snowContainer = document.getElementById(&quot;snow-container&quot;);

        // Función para ajustar la altura del contenedor al final de la página
        function expandToPageHeight() {
            const pageHeight = document.documentElement.scrollHeight; // Altura total de la página
            snowContainer.style.height = `${pageHeight}px`; // Establece el alto del contenedor hasta el final de la página
        }

        // Llamada inicial para ajustar la altura
        expandToPageHeight();

        // Asegurarse de que la altura se ajuste también cuando el usuario redimensione la ventana
        window.addEventListener(&quot;resize&quot;, expandToPageHeight);
    });
</script>

<script>
  document.addEventListener(&quot;DOMContentLoaded&quot;, function () {
    const mainBanner = document.getElementById(&quot;mainBanner&quot;);
    const hideBanner = document.getElementById(&quot;hideBanner&quot;);
    const showBanner = document.getElementById(&quot;showBanner&quot;);

    if (!mainBanner || !hideBanner || !showBanner) {
      console.error(&quot;Um ou mais elementos do banner não foram encontrados.&quot;);
      return;
    }

    function getCurrentDate() {
      const today = new Date();
      return `${today.getFullYear()}-${String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, &#39;0&#39;)}-${String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, &#39;0&#39;)}`;
    }

    const lastShown = localStorage.getItem(&quot;bannerLastShown&quot;);
    const currentDate = getCurrentDate();

    if (!lastShown || lastShown !== currentDate) {
      mainBanner.style.display = &quot;flex&quot;;
      showBanner.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
      localStorage.setItem(&quot;bannerLastShown&quot;, currentDate);
    } else {
      mainBanner.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
      showBanner.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
    }

    hideBanner.addEventListener(&quot;click&quot;, function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      mainBanner.classList.add(&quot;hidden-custom-banner&quot;);
      mainBanner.addEventListener(
        &quot;transitionend&quot;,
        function () {
          mainBanner.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
          showBanner.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
        },
        { once: true }
      );
    });

    showBanner.addEventListener(&quot;click&quot;, function () {
      mainBanner.style.display = &quot;flex&quot;;
      mainBanner.offsetHeight;
      mainBanner.classList.remove(&quot;hidden-custom-banner&quot;);
      showBanner.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
    });
  });
</script>
